With its rich leather upper and Western-inspired perforations, this dress shoe communicates a strong sense of style and of self. Dust bag included.</p>                                       <p>Put that final polish on your business look with the Strand wingtip oxford from Allen Edmonds. The perforation detail along the calf leather upper lends a distinguished air. Shankless construction eliminates the need for a break-in period for a comfortable fit right from the start. 360 welt construction binds the upper, footbed, and sole all the way around the shoe for extraordinary durability, flexibility, and comfort. The contoured last, designed to mimic men's feet, creates the perfect fit. The full leather lining is soft and breathable, while the premium oak leather sole flexes naturally with the foot.</p>                                                         <a class="a-link-normal" href="/dp/product-description/B001TDL0GK/ref=dp_proddesc_0?ie=UTF8&n=672123011&s=shoes">             See all Product Description</a>              </div>                                                                 </div>                                                                            </div>     <div id="detailBullets" class="feature" data-feature-name="detailBullets">                                                                                        <div id="detailBulletsWrapper_feature_div" data-feature-name="detailBullets" data-template-name="detailBullets" class="a-section a-spacing-none feature">     <div id="detailBullets_feature_div">                                <ul class="a-nostyle a-vertical a-spacing-none">                                       <li><span class="a-list-item">                     <span class="a-text-bold">ASIN:                     </span>                     <span>B001TDL0GK</span>                 </span></li>                              <li><span class="a-list-item">                     <span class="a-text-bold">Product Dimensions:                     </span>                     <span>12 x 8 x 4 inches;            <h3 class="a-spacing-small">Most Helpful Customer Reviews</h3> <div id="revMHRL" class="a-section">                            <div id="rev-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R1BS8O25OUWDQM" class="a-section celwidget"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro"><span class="a-size-small a-color-secondary">31 of 32 people found the following review helpful</span><div class="a-icon-row a-spacing-none"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" title="5.0 out of 5 stars" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R1BS8O25OUWDQM/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/183-5196858-4597147?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B001TDL0GK&nodeID=1036592&store=apparel"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-5"></i></a><span class="a-letter-space"></span><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R1BS8O25OUWDQM/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/183-5196858-4597147?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B001TDL0GK&nodeID=1036592&store=apparel"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">The Best</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">         <span class="a-size-normal">     <span class="a-color-secondary">       By     </span>     <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/A3D92E9KPRYMPY/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/183-5196858-4597147" class="noTextDecoration">Craig Newcomb</a>   </span> <span class="a-color-secondary"> on August 10, 2011</span></span></div><div id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R1BS8O25OUWDQM" class="a-row a-spacing-small">        <div class="a-section">   These are the best shoes I have ever owned. I own Cole Haan, Hugo Boss, Clarks, and Gordon Rush - all of those shoes feel cheap now. The Strand's are comfortable, look amazing, and are exceptionally high quality. I am so impressed with Allen Edmond that I intend to replace my lesser shoes with AE over the next few years. AE do go on sale (I purchased mine for a little under $200), so if the price is steep, just keep your eye open for sales. Also, I recommend you splurge on a nice shoe horn (like a <a class="a-link-normal" href="http://www.amazon.com/19-Shoe-Horn-Flexible-Classic/dp/B000KL7HHS/ref=cm_cr_dp_asin_lnk/183-5196858-4597147">19" Shoe Horn</a>), and a good set of cedar shoe trees, these shoes deserve to be treated well. I have purchased them through Amazon, Nordstrom, and directly from Allen-Edmonds (online, and brick and mortar stores). I have done this as 5 of the 8 purchased pairs had to be returned. Why? Because the heels were either slightly seperating brand new out of the box, or they were practically hanging off after 1-3 wears! I have come to the conclusion that no matter where you purchase Allen Edmonds shoes you will have this problem. I have also returned one to Nordstrom as the "broguing" on the shoe wasn't finished properly, the leather didn't terminate into a seam, it just stopped. And that bit of leather wasn't the same consistency color-wise. Quality control seems to be a problem, especially in the heel department! I kept 3 pairs that were up to snuff, but 3 good pairs out of 8 sold is not a good ratio! Allen-Edmonds for some reason has a great reputation. Perhaps it's because they are made in the USA (part of the reason I bought them), or they may have a great Marketing department. After having given their shoes a fair try multiple times, I have decided to look elsewhere for quality American-made shoes. I might save up a little more money, and give Alden a try. </div>  </div>             <a class="a-link-normal comment-link" title="2" These shoes are true to fit and for those looking for a narrow size this style can be found in A, B or C widths, at least from Allen Edmonds if they are not available here. Actually, the width range is from A to EEE but B & C widths start at size 8 and A widths at size 9. I normally wear size 9C but tried the 9B as I was able to get them at a very good price. The 9B fits comfortably snug (more so than a C width at the arch but not tight across the toes) and therefore offers great arch support.<br><br>The leather is top grade and takes a great shine. The style is timeless so they offer a sound purchase so long as you are not wanting to change with every fashion trend that comes along. The cushioning is hot cork but the shoes do not need additional padding because of the superior design. When walking I feel a sense of balance that I have not had with other brands as everything seems to be cut to precise proportions.<br><br>The style is great for business / dress occasions but can be dressed down with chinos etc. The perforated cap toe gives a look that is between a wing tip and a regular cap toe. The Strand now  has a MSRP of $325.00 so anything less is a deal. </div>  </div>        <a class="a-link-normal comment-link" title="1"
